## Idea

The construction of [morphisms of arrows](foundation.morphisms-arrows.md) is
functorial. We have a functorial action on pairs of
[morphisms of arrows](foundation.morphisms-arrows.md)

```text
  (α : f' ⇒ f, β : g ⇒ g') ↦ α ⇒ β : (f ⇒ g) → (f' ⇒ g')
```

We construct this functorial action as the restriction of a more general action
on morphisms of _exponentiated cospan diagrams_ of the form:

```text
            - ∘ f           g ∘ -
   (B → Y) ------> (A → Y) <------ (A → X)
      |               |               |
      |               |               |
      ∨     - ∘ f'    ∨    g' ∘ -     ∨
  (B' → Y') ----> (A' → Y') <---- (A' → X').
```

In general, such morphisms need not necessarily come from pairs of morphisms of
the underlying arrows.

This gives us a commuting triangle of functors

```text
  [pairs of arrows of types] ---> [exponentiated cospan diagrams]
                     \                 /
                      \               /
                       ∨             ∨
                      [arrows of types]
```

where the functorial action of morphisms of arrows is the left vertical arrow.

## Definitions

### The type of morphisms of arrows as a pullback

Given two maps `f : A → B` and `g : X → Y`, then the type of morphisms of arrows
from `f` to `g` is the pullback

```text
  hom-arrow f g ---------> (A → X)
        | ⌟                   |
        |                     | g ∘ -
        ∨                     ∨
     (B → Y) ------------> (A → Y).
                 - ∘ f
```

    <a id="5768" href="foundation.pullback-cones%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2029" class="Function">pullback-coneᵉ</a> <a id="5783" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3240" class="Function">cospan-diagram-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="5809" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5810" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3110" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="5814" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5816" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3114" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="5820" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5822" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3118" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="5826" href="Agda.Primitive.html#961" class="Primitive Operator">⊔</a> <a id="5828" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3122" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a><a id="5831" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="5835" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5737" class="Function">pullback-cone-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="5860" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="5866" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="5868" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5869" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1699" class="Function">hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="5880" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3200" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="5883" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3215" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="5886" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5889" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3698" class="Function">cone-hom-arrow&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="5905" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5907" href="foundation.dependent-pair-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#788" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,ᵉ</a> <a id="5910" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5464" class="Function">is-pullback-hom-arrowᵉ</a><a id="5932" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The bifunctorial map on morphisms of arrows inducing morphisms of the associated cospan diagrams of morphisms of arrows

Given morphisms of arrows `F : f' → f` and `G : g → g'`:

```text
            F₀                        G₀
      A' -------> A             X --------> X'
      |           |             |           |
   f' |     F     | f   and   g |     G     | g'
      ∨           ∨             ∨           ∨
      B' -------> B             Y --------> Y',
            F₁                        G₁
```

there is an associated morphism of cospan diagrams

```text
              - ∘ f           g ∘ -
     (B → Y) ------> (A → Y) <------ (A → X)
        |               |               |
        |               |               |
  (F₁ ∘ - ∘ G₁)   (G₁ ∘ - ∘ F₀)   (G₀ ∘ - ∘ F₀)
        |               |               |
        ∨     - ∘ f'    ∨    g' ∘ -     ∨
    (B' → Y') ----> (A' → Y') <---- (A' → X')
```

and this construction is bifunctorial.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="6909" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6916" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6916" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="6920" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6921" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6921" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="6925" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6925" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="6929" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6929" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="6933" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6933" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="6937" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6937" class="Bound">l1&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="6942" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6942" class="Bound">l2&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="6947" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6947" class="Bound">l3&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="6952" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#6952" class="Bound">l4&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="6957" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6959" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="6964" class="Symbol">}</a>

### The functorial action on morphisms of cospan diagrams of morphisms of arrows

<pre class="Agda"><a id="7740" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="7747" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7747" class="Module">_</a>

### The functorial action of morphisms of arrows on cospan diagrams preserves identities

<pre class="Agda"><a id="18170" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="18177" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18177" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="18181" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18182" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18182" class="Bound">l1ᵉ</a> <a id="18186" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18186" class="Bound">l2ᵉ</a> <a id="18190" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18190" class="Bound">l3ᵉ</a> <a id="18194" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#18194" class="Bound">l4ᵉ</a> <a id="18198" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18200" href="Agda.Primitive.html#742" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="18205" class="Symbol">}</a>

        <a id="19726" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="19728" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19359" class="Bound">h&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="19731" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="19734" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#2800" class="Function Operator">~ᵉ</a>
    <a id="19741" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8008" class="Function">map-hom-arrow-hom-cospan-diagramᵉ</a> <a id="19775" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19082" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="19779" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19100" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="19783" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19120" class="Bound">f&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="19788" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19141" class="Bound">g&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="19793" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19228" class="Bound">hᵉ</a> <a id="19796" href="foundation-core.function-types%25E1%25B5%2589.html#476" class="Function Operator">∘ᵉ</a>

        <a id="20907" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="20909" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20634" class="Bound">h&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="20912" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="20915" class="Symbol">→</a>

    <a id="20979" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8008" class="Function">map-hom-arrow-hom-cospan-diagramᵉ</a> <a id="21013" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20426" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="21016" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20441" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="21019" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20528" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="21023" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20546" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="21027" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20634" class="Bound">h&#39;ᵉ</a>
  <a id="21033" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20574" class="Function">preserves-htpy-map-hom-arrow-hom-cospan-diagramᵉ</a> <a id="21082" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="21088" href="foundation.functoriality-pullbacks%25E1%25B5%2589.html#9727" class="Function">preserves-htpy-map-pullback-coneᵉ</a>
      <a id="21128" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21130" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3240" class="Function">cospan-diagram-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="21156" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20426" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="21159" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20441" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="21161" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21169" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21171" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3240" class="Function">cospan-diagram-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="21197" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20528" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="21201" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20546" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="21204" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21212" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21214" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5737" class="Function">pullback-cone-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="21239" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20426" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="21242" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20441" class="Bound">gᵉ</a><a id="21244" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="21252" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="21254" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#5737" class="Function">pullback-cone-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="21279" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20528" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="21283" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20546" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="21286" class="Symbol">)</a>
</pre>
### The bifunctorial action of morphisms of arrows preserves identities

**Proof.** This follows by the fact that functors compose.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="21434" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="21441" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#21441" class="Module">_</a>

  <a id="21567" class="Keyword">where</a>

### The bifunctorial action of morphisms of arrows preserves composition

**Proof.** This follows by the fact that functors compose.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="22218" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="22225" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22225" class="Module">_</a>

        <a id="23516" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23518" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7177" class="Function">map-hom-cospan-diagram-hom-arrowsᵉ</a> <a id="23553" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22512" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="23556" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22527" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="23559" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22544" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23563" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22562" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23567" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23029" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="23570" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23040" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="23572" class="Symbol">))</a>
      <a id="23581" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23583" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#17010" class="Function">preserves-comp-map-hom-cospan-diagram-hom-arrowsᵉ</a>
          <a id="23643" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22512" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="23646" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22527" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="23649" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22544" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23653" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22562" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23657" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22582" class="Bound">f&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23662" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22603" class="Bound">g&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23667" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23029" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="23670" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23032" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23674" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23036" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23678" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23040" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="23680" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="23683" href="foundation-core.homotopies%25E1%25B5%2589.html#3445" class="Function Operator">∙hᵉ</a>
    <a id="23691" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23693" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#19172" class="Function">preserves-comp-map-hom-arrow-hom-cospan-diagramᵉ</a> <a id="23742" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22512" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="23745" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22527" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="23748" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22544" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23752" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22562" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23756" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22582" class="Bound">f&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23761" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22603" class="Bound">g&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a>
      <a id="23772" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23774" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7177" class="Function">map-hom-cospan-diagram-hom-arrowsᵉ</a> <a id="23809" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22544" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23813" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22562" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23817" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22582" class="Bound">f&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23822" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22603" class="Bound">g&#39;&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23827" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23032" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23831" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23036" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="23834" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="23842" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="23844" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#7177" class="Function">map-hom-cospan-diagram-hom-arrowsᵉ</a> <a id="23879" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22512" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="23882" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22527" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="23885" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22544" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23889" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#22562" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="23893" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23029" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="23896" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#23040" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a><a id="23898" class="Symbol">))</a>
</pre>
### The bifunctorial action of morphisms of arrows preserves homotopies

**Proof.** This follows by the fact that functors compose.

<pre class="Agda"><a id="24047" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="24054" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24054" class="Module">_</a>

  <a id="24168" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24169" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24169" class="Bound">A&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24173" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24175" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="24179" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24075" class="Bound">l1&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="24183" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24185" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24186" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24186" class="Bound">B&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24190" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24192" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="24196" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24080" class="Bound">l2&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="24200" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24202" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24203" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24203" class="Bound">X&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24207" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24209" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="24213" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24085" class="Bound">l3&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="24217" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="24219" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="24220" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24220" class="Bound">Y&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24224" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24226" href="Agda.Primitive.html#429" class="Primitive">UUᵉ</a> <a id="24230" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24090" class="Bound">l4&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="24234" class="Symbol">}</a>

  <a id="24306" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="24315" class="Keyword">abstract</a>
    <a id="24328" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24328" class="Function">preserves-htpy-map-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="24358" class="Symbol">:</a>
      <a id="24366" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24367" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24367" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="24370" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24370" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24374" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24376" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1699" class="Function">hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="24387" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24269" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24391" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24239" class="Bound">fᵉ</a><a id="24393" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24395" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="24396" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24396" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="24399" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24399" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24403" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="24405" href="foundation.morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#1699" class="Function">hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="24416" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24254" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="24419" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24287" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a><a id="24422" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="24424" class="Symbol">→</a>

      <a id="24546" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#8760" class="Function">map-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="24561" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24239" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="24564" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24254" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="24567" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24269" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24571" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24287" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24575" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24370" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24579" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24399" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a>
    <a id="24587" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24328" class="Function">preserves-htpy-map-hom-arrowᵉ</a> <a id="24617" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24617" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="24620" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24620" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24624" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24624" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="24627" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24627" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24631" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24631" class="Bound">HFᵉ</a> <a id="24635" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24635" class="Bound">HGᵉ</a> <a id="24639" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="24647" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#20574" class="Function">preserves-htpy-map-hom-arrow-hom-cospan-diagramᵉ</a> <a id="24696" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24239" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="24699" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24254" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="24702" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24269" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24706" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24287" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a>

            <a id="24916" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24239" class="Bound">fᵉ</a> <a id="24919" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24254" class="Bound">gᵉ</a> <a id="24922" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24269" class="Bound">f&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24926" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24287" class="Bound">g&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24930" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24617" class="Bound">Fᵉ</a> <a id="24933" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24620" class="Bound">F&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24937" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24624" class="Bound">Gᵉ</a> <a id="24940" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24627" class="Bound">G&#39;ᵉ</a> <a id="24944" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24631" class="Bound">HFᵉ</a> <a id="24948" href="foundation.functoriality-morphisms-arrows%25E1%25B5%2589.html#24635" class="Bound">HGᵉ</a><a id="24951" class="Symbol">)</a>
